Abstract—The novel feature extraction method for 
nonintrusive load monitoring (NILM) systems was proposed 
in this paper.  In order to monitoring the status of each load, 
a sensor is installed for each load traditionally.  The status of 
the load is transmitted to the main controller such that the 
status of each load can be monitored.  On the other hand, the 
NILM is able to detect the status of loads by analyzing the 
current signals that is picked-up by a current sensor 
installed at the main electrical panel. 
Traditional NILM methods used real power, reactive 
power, harmonic contents of power signatures and transient 
energy to determine the status of appliances.  These methods 
are very complex and require a lot of computation.  In this 
paper, a novel method that integrates artificial intelligent 
recognition technique and load current acquisition method 
for NILM is proposed. The proposed method uses time-
domain information.  This approach is different from 
traditional NILM methods. The proposed method is able to 
detect the energization and de-energization of loads by 
applying back-propagation neural networks (BP-ANNs).  
The overall correct rate for this method is above 98.75%.  
This result shows that the proposed method is able to 
determine the operation status of loads with proper 
robustness. 
Keywords-Feature extraction; Back-propagation neural 
network; Nonintrusive load monitoring; Power signatures 
I.  INTRODUCTION 
Detection of the usage of loads in a house is an import 
problem recently due to higher cost of fossil energy.  In 
order to conserve the energy, several polices were 
proposed by the government.  The most important step to 
conserve the energy is realizing how the energy is used in 
a house.  The easiest way of detection the usage of energy 
can be achieved by installing sensors for each load. The 
sensors send the power usage information to the control 
device in order to keep track the usage of energy for each 
device.  However, this method requires a large amount of 
sensors.  On the other hand, the nonintrusive load 
monitoring (NILM) method requires a set of current and 
voltage sensors that are installed at the main electrical 
panel.  By analyzing the current and voltage waveforms, 
the power usage of each load can be detected.  Compared 
with traditional technique, the NILM has several 
advantages, e.g., easier to install, lower cost, lower energy 
consumption, etc.  Several methods that implement NILM 
were proposed [1-10]. 
In this paper, a new method that is different from other 
NILM methods is proposed.  The method integrates load 
current acquisition method and artificial recognition 
technique.  The transient wave form as well as steady-state 
wave form is acquired.  The features are extracted from the 
acquired wave forms.  A pattern recognition system is used.  
A real scenario is used to test the robustness of the 
proposed method.  The results of the test show that the 
proposed method is able to identify different loads when 
they are operated at the same time. 
The organization of the paper is as following.  First, the 
existing methods and power wave form features used by 
these methods are discussed.  The proposed NILM method 
is discussed in Sec. 3.  The laboratory test and 
experimental results are shown in Sec. 4.  A popular 
recognizer that is used for load usage recognitions are also 
discussed in Sec. 4.  The results and conclusions are 
discussed in Sec. 5. 
II. THE CHARACTERISTICS OF POWER WAVE FORMS 
Two major research topics on NILM were focused on 
the usage of steady-state and transient analysis.  For the 
steady-state analysis, an NILM system was developed by 
the Electric Power Research Institute (EPRI) [1].  The 
system uses the variations of real and reactive power to 
detect the status of loads based on the P-Q plane. 
Although this method had been applied to some regular 
houses with acceptable performance, several problems 
were pointed out by papers [2-4].  In papers [5, 6], 
nonlinear loads not only consumes real and reactive power, 
they also introduce harmonics to the power lines.  This 
harmonics can be used as features to detect different loads.  
Besides the usage of steady-state analysis, the research 
team led by Steve Leeb pointed out that the transient wave 
forms are different for different loads due to the 
differences of physical characteristics [2, 3, 7, 8].  
Therefore, the transient characteristics can also be used for 
the load recognition.  Besides the discovery of the transient 
characteristics, they also found that these transient wave 
forms have complete or partial repeatability.  By applying 
short-term Fast-Fourier Transform (frequency domain), the

Design and Implementation of Flexible Power 
Interfaces for Distributed Generators 
Tsao-Tsung Ma 
Dept. of Electrical Engineering, CEECS 
National United University 
MiaoLi City 36003, Taiwan 
tonyma@nuu.edu.tw
Jer-Yih Su 
Dept. of Electrical Engineering, CEECS 
National United University 
MiaoLi City 36003, Taiwan 
m9821009@smail.nuu.edu.tw
Abstract—This paper describes a novel design concept of power 
interfaces connecting distributed generators (DG) to the 
distribution networks. The proposed power interface is able to 
perform multiple compensating functions besides regulating the 
real power fed from DG systems. The hardware structure used in 
the proposed system is similar to the conventional static 
synchronous compensator (STATCOM), a converter-based 
flexible ac transmission systems (FACTS) device; however, its 
power rating is designed at the distribution level to facilitate the 
used of pulse width modulation techniques. With the proposed 
control scheme, the key control functions of distribution 
STATCOM and active power filters (APF) can be integrated into 
a single DG hardware system. To demonstrate the feasibility of 
the proposed control scheme, performances in compensating load 
current harmonics and the reactive power compensation of the 
system are investigated. The feasibility and effectiveness of the 
proposed flexible power interface are verified by simulations and 
laboratory tests. 
Keywords- Distributed generator; flexible ac transmission 
systems; reactive power compensation; active power filter
I. INTRODUCTION
Advanced control algorithms and power electronics are key 
technologies for enabling renewable power generation and 
operating the distribution networks with improved 
controllability and efficiency. The DG system is normally 
defined as an electric power source connected directly to the 
distribution network or on the customer side [1]. These 
distributed energy sources can be cogeneration system with 
micro turbine (MT), fuel cell (FC), photovoltaic (PV), wind 
turbine (WT) or any combination of the above renewable 
energy sources. In recent years, many studies have indicated 
that DG will play a significant role in the future power systems. 
A study by Electric Power Research Institute (EPRI) indicates 
that by 2010, about 25% of the new power generation will be 
the form of distributed energy sources [2-3]. Another study by 
the National Gas Foundation concluded that this figure could 
be even as high as 30% [4].  It has been well accepted that the 
integration of DG systems with the utility distribution network 
offers a number of technical, environmental and economic 
benefits. It also gives a great opportunity for distribution 
utilities to improve the performance of networks in terms of 
power losses, voltage stability and reliability [5-6]. However, 
there are a number of technical challenges associated with the 
successful application of DG systems. Of these challenges, the 
design of proper power interface systems connecting the DG to 
the grid is one of the crucial tasks.  This paper focuses on the 
investigation of a simple integrated power interface system 
based on a three-phase inverter structure and a simple current 
hysteresis controller, which make the control functions among 
the grid, local load and DG can be flexible and a cost-effective 
system can be achieved. 
In the aspects of compensation functions, reactive power 
compensation is an important issue in the control of 
distribution voltages. Reactive current supplied by the grid 
increases the distribution system losses, reduces the system 
power factor. It also limits the active power capability of the 
feeder and can even cause large variations in the load-side 
voltages [6].  In some cases, rapid changes in the reactive 
power consumption of large loads can cause voltage 
oscillations, e.g., flickers in the case of arc furnaces.  
Theoretically, the connection of DG to the distribution systems 
has significant impact on the flow of real power and voltage 
conditions on both utility and customer sides. To eliminate or 
release some of these adverse impacts, this paper proposes a 
multi-functional power interface (MFPI) for DG systems. 
Beside the main function of regulating the active power 
supplied from DG to the utility, the proposed MFPI can also 
supply reactive power to the utility to enable a desired power 
factor operation or to regulate the voltage at the point of 
common coupling (PCC). In addition, it is our intention to 
make the MFPI can be controlled in a manner to compensate 
the harmonics generated from nonlinear loads and mitigate 
different power quality problems like sags, swells and even 
unbalance. It is worthwhile to note that the proposed MFPI can 
perform the function of real power regulation of DG and 
simultaneously solve most of the distribution system problems, 
which are presently handled by various existing compensation 
devices. 
In this paper, current controlled voltage source inverter 
(VSI) is used for the design of MFPI. The command signals for 
the VSI, which is current signal in nature, will include the 
information of active power supplied from DG system and the 
integrated component of current harmonics and reactive power

1126 IEEE TRANSACTIONS ON POWER SYSTEMS, VOL. 25, NO. 2, MAY 2010
Application of Grey Correlation Analysis
in Evolutionary Programming for Distribution
System Feeder Reconfiguration
Men-Shen Tsai, Member, IEEE, and Fu-Yuan Hsu
Abstract—Feeder reconfiguration is a common technique that
is used by distribution system operators during normal or emer-
gency operational planning. By changing the status of switches on
the distribution systems, the feeders can be reconfigured. During
a feeder reconfiguration, more than one objective is considered
by the distribution system operators. Due to the complexity of
the reconfiguration problems, the system operators are looking
for assistance from computer program that can provide adequate
switching plans to reconfigure the feeders such that the desired
goal can be achieved. Thus, the feeder reconfiguration is a type
of discrete multi-objective optimization problems. Evolutionary
programming (EP) technique is a method that can be applied
to identify an optimal switching plan for feeder reconfiguration.
A fitness function is required in EP for chromosome selection
during reproduction process. The fitness function needs to inte-
grate the objectives to provide a measure for each chromosome.
Normalizing the objectives is a typical method for multi-objective
optimizations such that these objectives are comparable. In this
paper, Gray CoRrelation Analysis (GCRA) method is proposed.
The proposed method is used to integrate the objectives and pro-
vide a relative measure to a particular switching plan associated
with a chromosome without any prior knowledge of the system
under reconfiguration. Two different distribution systems are used
in this paper to demonstrate how the proposed GCRA is applied
during the selection process of EP. Several simulations show that
the EP can identify the solution more accurately when GCRA is
applied than other methods.
Index Terms—Evolutionary programming, grey correlation
analysis, power distribution planning.
I. INTRODUCTION
T HE power distribution system is formed by many inter-connected feeders with normally open tie switches and
normally closed sectionalized switches. The feeder reconfigu-
ration is used by power distribution operators to alleviate prob-
lems during normal or emergency operations by changing the
structure of the feeders. The radial structure of power distri-
bution systems must be maintained and all non-failure zones
must be kept energized during the feeder reconfiguration. More-
over, several criterions are considered simultaneously when the
Manuscript received May 15, 2008; revised January 05, 2009. First published
November 17, 2009; current version published April 21, 2010. This work was
supported by the National Science Council of the Republic of China under Con-
tract NSC 94-2213-E-027-051. Paper no. TPWRS-00404-2008.
The authors are with the Graduate Institute of Automation Technology, Na-
tional Taipei University of Technology, Taipei, Taiwan (e-mail: mstsai@ntut.
edu.tw; s3669016@ntut.edu.tw).
Color versions of one or more of the figures in this paper are available online
at http://ieeexplore.ieee.org.
Digital Object Identifier 10.1109/TPWRS.2009.2032325
feeder reconfiguration is performed by distribution system oper-
ators. Traditional optimizationmethodologiesmay not provide a
suitable solution for feeder reconfiguration within a limited time
due to the special constraints of distribution system structure.
Therefore, heuristic methods such as expert system [1], fuzzy
logic [2], [3], Tabu search [4], [5], genetic algorithm (GA)/evo-
lutional programming (EP) [6]–[11], particle swarm optimiza-
tion (PSO) [12], [13], ant colony optimization (ACO) [14]–[17],
etc. were proposed in the past.
During reconfiguration of distribution feeders, several ob-
jectives are considered by the distribution system operators.
These objectives include: 1) line losses [1], [4], [6]–[11], [13],
[18]–[20], [22], [24]; 2) load balancing [4], [5], [11], [20], [21],
[23], [24]; 3) voltage drop [2], [3], [5], [8], [9], [24]; 4) number
of switching actions [2], [3], [8], [9]; etc. Single objective
optimization was considered in the past. However, since these
objectives are all important, the system operators may want
to consider several objectives simultaneously, i.e., minimize
the power losses with minimum number of switch operations
during reconfiguration. By considering multi-objectives, the
distribution system operators can operate the distribution
system in a more economic way while the system can be
maintained in safer operation conditions. In 1996, Roytelman
published a paper that considered multi-objectives during
feeder reconfiguration [24]. Since then, the multi-objective
feeder reconfiguration had become an important research issue
[2], [3], [5], [8], [9], [11].
In order to utilizing the existing optimization techniques,
integrating several objectives into single objective is needed.
Unfortunately, the objectives cannot be integrated directly due
to their characteristics. Normalization of these objectives is
needed. Weighted sum [5], [13], [25] and fuzzy rule-based
[2], [3], [8], [9] methods were proposed to normalize the
objectives. By applying these techniques, the objectives are
comparable and can be integrated. However, identifying the
normalization parameters in weighted sum method is a difficult
task since the characteristics of objectives are different. For
fuzzy rule-based methods, the construction of the membership
functions is the key issue for quantifying the objectives. These
membership functions vary for different systems. The degree of
the membership functions of objectives will be changed at dif-
ferent operating conditions as well. Therefore, the membership
functions need to be modified accordingly. Grey CoRrelation
Analysis (GCRA) is proposed in this paper to integrate the
objectives and provide a value to represent the fitness of a
solution without any prior knowledge of the objectives. Four
objectives during feeder reconfiguration are considered in this
paper: load balance, power losses, percentage of voltage drop,
and the number of switching actions. Two distribution systems
are used to verify the feasibility and evaluate the performance

2 月 21 日 (星期一)：參加 ISSCC2011 。 
 
今年的大會主題為 Electronics for Healthy Living。上午 8:15-12:00 為 planery session 除頒
發相關獎項及證書外，有三場演講及一場技術圓桌會議：第一場原由 Medtronic Senior
的 VP Stephen oesterle 講演 New Interfaces to the Body Through implantable System 
integration，但由於大雪班機延誤不能到場改由同事代為講演；第二場是由 imec/Holst 
Centre 的 Senior VP Jo de Boeck 講演 Game-Changing Opportunities for Wireless Personal 
Healthcare and Lifestyle；第三場是由三星電子的總經理 oh-hyun Kwon 講演 Eco-Friendly 
Semiconductor Technologies for Healthy Living；接下來為由 University of California, 
Berkeley 的 Jan Rabaey 教授主持的 Technology Roundtable（ISSCC 第一屆技術圓桌會議）
主題為 Beyond the Horizon: The next 10x Reduction in Power - Challenges and Solutions。
下午 1:30-5:15 聆聽在 Session 2: Technologies for Health 發表的八篇論文。晚上 8:00-10:00
參加由鈺創科技董事長盧超群博士主持的 Evening Session 3: Future System and Memory 
architectures: Transformations by Technology and applications。 
 
2 月 22 日 (星期二)：ISSCC2011。 
 
上午 8:30-12:15 聆聽在 Session 11: Non-Volatile Memory Solutions 發表的八篇論文。計有
Toshiba 和 Sandisk 發表的 A 151mm2 64Gb MLC nand Flash Memory in 24nm CMOS 
Technology；我們（工研院、清華與中央）發表的 A 4Mb Embedded SLC Resistive-RAM 
Macro with 7.2ns Read-Write Random-Access Time and 160ns MLC-Access Capability；
Hynix Semiconductor 發 表 的 A 32Gb MLC NAND Flash Memory with Vth 
Margin-Expanding Schemes in 26nm CMOS；University of Tokyo 發表的 95%-Lower-BER 
43%-Lower-Power Intelligent Solid-State Drive (SSD) with Asymmetric Coding and Stripe 
Pattern Elimination Algorithm；清華與 Fukuoka Institute of Technology 發表由張孟凡教授
講 演 的  An Offset-Tolerant Current-Sampling-Based Sense Amplifier for 
Sub-100nA-Cell-Current Nonvolatile Memory；Massachusetts Institute of Technology 發表的
A low-voltage 1Mb FeRAM in 0.13μm CMOS Featuring Time-to-Digital Sensing for 
Expanded Operating Margin in Scaled CMOS；Sony 發表的 A 4Mb Conductive-Bridge 
Resistive Memory with 2.3GB/s Read-Throughput and 216MB/s Program-Throughput；
Samsung Electronics 發表的 A 7MB/s 64Gb 3-Bit/cell DDR NAND Flash Memory in 
20nm-Node Technology。下午 1:30-3:15 聆聽在 Session 12: Design in Emerging Technologies
發表的四篇論文。下午 3:15-5:15 聆聽在 Session 16: mm-Wave Design Techniques 發表的
四篇論文。傍晚 5:15-7:00 參加今年新增的 Industry Demonstration Session。晚上 8:00-10:00
參加由由Gigle Networks Jed hurwitz主持的 Evening Session 5: Technologies for Smart Grid 
and Smart Meter。 
 
2 月 23 日 (星期三)：ISSCC2011 。 
五、建議 
ISSCC 是電子電路領域最重要的指標國際研討會，由 IEEE Solid-StateCircuit 學會主辦。在這
會議中，來自全球頂尖的實驗室（大學及研究機構）展示他們一年來電子電路最新的研究成
果。參加這個會議可以瞭解目前電子電路的發展趨勢，也可以和來自世界各地的電子電路專
家相互切磋。我們應多多鼓勵學門同仁參與此會議以提升在電子電路的研究能量。

12 月 7 日 (星期二)：參加 iedm2010 。 
 
上午 9:00-12:00聆聽在 Session 13: Emerging Technologies – Next Generation Power Devices 
and Technology 發表的六篇論文。計有 Texas Instruments 的 Philip Hower 講演 Current 
Status and Future Trends in Silicon Power Devices，University of California, Santa Barbara 的
U. Mishra 講演 AlGaN/GaN Transistors for Power Electronics，KTH Royal Institute of 
Technology and TranSiC AB 的 M. Ostling 講演 Silicon Carbide based Power Devices，ABB 
Switzerland, Ltd.的 M. Rahimo 講演 Ultra High Voltage Semiconductor Power Devices for 
Grid Applications，T Toyota Central R&D Labs 的 M. Kanechika 講演 Advanced SiC and

and Directions for Mobile Wireless Devices 講演。下午 2:15-5:15 聆聽在 Session 19: Memory

題為 Heterogeneous Device Integration as Enabler of Functional Diversification for More than 
Moore。 
 
12 月 8 日 (星期三)：參加 iedm2010 。 
 
上午 9:00-12:00 聆聽在 Session 27: CMOS Devices and Technology – Advanced High-k 
Metal Gate SoC and High Performance CMOS Platforms，Session 28: Characterization, 
Reliability, and Yield – RTN and Memory 及 Session 29: Memory Technology – Phase Change 
Memory and 3-Dimensional Memory 發表的七篇論文。下午 1:30-4:00 聆聽在 Session 34: 
CMOS Devices and Technology – Advanced FinFETs and Nanowire FETs 發表的六篇論文。 
 
12 月 9 日 (星期四)：離開舊金山。 
Fully Featured 22/20nm Technology Platform from TSMC -- TSMC will unveil a complete 
high-performance 22/20nm CMOS logic technology at IEDM 2010. It features FinFET 
transistor architectures, aggressive 193nm immersion lithography, SiGe stressors, metal gates 
and high-k dielectrics. The FinFETs, built with dual-epitaxy and multiple stressors, demonstrate 
outstanding performance in both n- and p-channel versions, enabling maximum design 
flexibility. N-/P-channel on-current is 1200/1100µA/µm respectively, while off-current for both 
N and P versions is 100nA/µm. The researchers used the new technology to build a dense 
0.1µm2 SRAM memory cell, which had excellent noise characteristics (90mV noise margin) 
even at a low 0.45V operating voltage.

五、建議 
iedm 是電子元件領域最重要的國際研討會，也是 IEEE Electron Device 學會的年會。在這
會議中，來自全球頂尖的實驗室（大學及研究機構）展示他們一年來電子元件最新的研
究成果。參加這個會議可以瞭解目前電子元件的發展趨勢，也可以和來自世界各地的電
子元件專家相互切磋。我們應多多鼓勵學門同仁參與此會議以提升在電子元件的研究能
量。 
 
  
 
 二、心得 
 
學生在澳洲當地參加此次 International minigrids workshop 之外，也在會中結識許
多國外學者，包含澳洲當地的研究教授學者、日本研究機構的學者等等，和這些學者的交談
也讓學生受益良多。 
 
    這次前往澳洲行程，學生感到非常地開心，可以和參與學生研究內容領域的相關研討
會，學生很珍惜有這樣的機會。除此之外，這次參訪行程，不僅拓展了學生的視野，並結識
了許多當地的學術研究者，相信這種經由學術連結起來的關係，未來會是學生的一項重要資
產。最後，感謝國科會的補助及行政人員的協助，使學生能夠順利成行。

國科會補助計畫衍生研發成果推廣資料表
日期:2011/10/14
國科會補助計畫
計畫名稱: 智慧型微電網示範系統之規劃、分析、設計、與建置
計畫主持人: 連振炘
計畫編號: 98-3114-E-007-004- 學門領域: 節能減碳技術分項計畫－智慧電
網與讀表－電力工程

項等，請以文字敘述填
列。) 
1. 所建立之切換式磁阻發電機系統、直流微電網、超級電容及鋰電池儲能系
統、單相三線式 220V/110V 變頻器等，具新穎性及良好操控性能，具有實用價
值，可供國內外微電網設計建立之參考。 
2. 已完成之智慧型多功能緊急電力控制器具觀念及技術之創新性。 
3. 本研究釐清微電網於不同供電方式下之故障電流特性，模擬結果具參考價
值。 
4. 已完成之微電網孤島運轉及併聯運轉分析，具保護協調規劃上之之實務價
值。 
5. 結合大氣物理與電機之跨領域合作

目 計畫成果推廣之參與（閱聽）人數 0  
 
階段，透過本研究在技術上的開發，可以將本國在多 
代理人於電網的研究層級與國際並駕齊驅。 
a. 經濟產業效益 
(1) 本研究所開發之雙饋感應發電機之無感測型控制策 
略、自主型轉換器控制技術及其動態模型的建立、微 
電網併網轉為孤島運轉之緊急控制策略可推廣至本國 
相關產業，增進產業效益。  
(2) 微電網於孤島運轉模式下智慧型多功能緊急電力控制 
器之規劃與智慧型控制器設計(EFPC_Shunt 部份) 
(3) 自主型轉換器控制技術及其動態模型的建立，可協助 
國內相關中小企業開發燃油引擎發電機組之相關技 
術，有助於未來朝向高功率轉換器領域的推進，對產 
業界長期的發展有相當的幫助。 
(4) 已完成之微電網併網轉為孤島運轉之緊急控制策略 
之研究(含 DG 端快速孤島偵測方法及併網與孤島之 
運轉模式轉換控制策略)具實際應用價值。 
 (5) 智慧電網將積極推動先進電錶系統(Advanced 
Metering Infrastucture)其中包含智慧型電錶，台灣目前 
有 23000 戶高壓用戶其用電量佔全台 50%，將優先安 
裝智慧型電錶，預計於 2011 年完成，進而於 10 年推 
廣至一般用戶，可望為台灣智慧型電錶產業帶來龐大 
商機。 
(6) 由於各國均高度重視智慧電網的發展，相關於智慧電 
網設備的開發也可以為本國相關產業提供另一個市 
場。由於目前使用的系統極為龐大，本國中小企業無 
力投入龐大經費進行系統開發，因此目前大部分的市 
場均由國外大型公司所獨佔。但由於分散式計算的興 
起，許多原先透過大型系統負責監控的方式，將會逐 
漸轉移為分散式的計算。此一改變有利於本國中小企 
業的研發與投入。本計畫開發的技術，在將來因智慧 
電網的需求，可以提供本國企業相關開發技術，讓本 
國產業可以快速研發相關產品。 
b. 社會效益 
(1) 本研究開發之 AlGaN/GaN HEMT 元件可以有效的增 
加電力轉換的效率，降低能量的損耗，可達能國家型 
能源計畫節能減碳的終極目標，減少社會成本支出。 
 (2) 本計劃進行之需求面能源整合系統軟硬體帄台之致能 
技術研究，運用電力需量控制技術，除了抑制實驗單 
位超約附加費外，更強化系統功能，與需量交易帄台
